If OBJECT_ID('U_Dsi_EquifaxCustom_Backup') IS NULL 
	CREATE TABLE dbo.U_Dsi_EquifaxCustom_Backup (
		 SP_NAME VARCHAR(50)
		,SP_CODE NVARCHAR(MAX)
		,DateCreated DATETIME );
If OBJECT_ID('dsi_sp_BuildDriverTables_EEQFX_Custom') IS NOT NULL 
	BEGIN	
		INSERT INTO dbo.U_Dsi_EquifaxCustom_Backup
		SELECT DISTINCT A.NAME AS SP_NAME, M.DEFINITION AS SP_Code, GETDATE()
		FROM SYS.SQL_MODULES M 
		INNER JOIN SYS.OBJECTS A ON M.OBJECT_ID = A.OBJECT_ID
		WHERE A.Name = 'dsi_sp_BuildDriverTables_EEQFX_Custom' AND  A.type = 'P';
	END
GO

  [tytdeeid] char(12)  NOT NULL ,
  [tytdeqcocode] varchar(15)  NULL ,
  [tytdlocation] char(6)  NULL ,
  [YTD_FUTA] money  NULL ,
  [YTD_EIC] money  NULL 
);
GO


/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[dsi_EEQFX_IncludeSQLClausesRecordSet]    Script Date: 08/02/2010 18:52:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON;
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON;
GO
create procedure [dbo].[dsi_EEQFX_IncludeSQLClausesRecordSet] (
@formatCode varchar(12), @RecordSet varchar(3), @useRecordSet varchar(1)
)
as
begin


 update u_dsi_sqlclauses set
  WhereClause =	case 
					when @useRecordSet = 'N' then 
					case when charindex('Ignore',ltrim(isnull(WhereClause,'')),1) <> 1 then 'Ignore' + isnull(WhereClause,'')
							else WhereClause end
					else 
					case 
						when charindex('Ignore',ltrim(isnull(WhereClause,'')),1) = 1 then substring(WhereClause,7,len(WhereClause) - 6)
						else WhereClause end
				end
 where
	formatcode = @formatCode -- 'EEQFX'
	and
	RecordSet = @RecordSet;
end
GO



/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[dsi_sp_BuildDriverTables_EEQFX_Custom]    Script Date: 08/02/2010 18:52:24 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON;
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON;
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[dsi_sp_BuildDriverTables_EEQFX_Custom]
@Custom varchar(15)
AS

/************************************************************

Created By: Diane Hendrix
Create Date: March 2015

Purpose: this module is used by Equifax clients for any custom code
	This module is also used if client is using the Benefits or I-9 modules


** Please note some clients have different Equifax company codes (drvcocode). 
 In such case data needs to be summed within the Equifax company. Also, client
may have different files created based on Equifax company. 
 There may also be override parameters or translations in u_dsi_translation_v2 to use.
If recordsets are in the translations, they are to not be processed, so query should not create 
records in the table.

There is a variable in the configuration to indicate if separate files are need by equifax company

UPDATE u_dsi_configuration SET cfgValue = dbo.dsi_fnVariable('EEQFX','UdesPath') WHERE FormatCode = 'EEQFX' AND CfgName LIKE '%ExportPath'
UPDATE u_dsi_configuration SET cfgValue = 'Y' WHERE FormatCode = 'EEQFX' AND CfgName = 'cCustom'  -- Y or N
UPDATE u_dsi_configuration SET cfgValue = 'P' WHERE FormatCode = 'EEQFX' AND CfgName = 'vFileType'   -- T or P
UPDATE u_dsi_configuration SET cfgValue = 'N' WHERE FormatCode = 'EEQFX' AND CfgName = 'Testing' -- Y or N


Revision History
-----------------
Updated By		Date			CP Num			Desc	



************************************************************/

	/***************************
	COLLECT DATE PARAMETERS
	****************************/
	DECLARE 
		@StartDate DATETIME,
		@EndDate DATETIME,
		@StartPerControl Char(9),
		@EndPerControl Char(9),
		@FormatCode Char(10),
		@ExportCode Char(10),
		@ExportFile char(200);
		

	SELECT 
		@StartDate = CONVERT(DATETIME, LEFT(StartPerControl, 8) ),
		@EndDate = CONVERT(DATETIME, LEFT(EndPerControl , 8)  ),
		@StartPerControl = startpercontrol,
		@EndPerControl  = endpercontrol,
		@FormatCode = formatcode,
		@ExportCode = Exportcode,
		@Exportfile = ExportFile
	FROM dbo.U_Dsi_Parameters 
	WHERE formatcode = 'EEQFX';

	declare @dummy char(1);

	/**********************************
	Custom Code for EELIST
	***********************************/
	
	if @Custom = 'EELIST'

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '';  --replace with custom code
	END


	/**********************************
	Custom Code for 202 Record
	***********************************/
	
	if @Custom = '202' 

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '';  --replace with custom code
	END


	/**********************************
	Custom Code for 210 Record
	***********************************/
	
	if @Custom = '210'

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '' ; --replace with custom code
	END


	/**********************************
	Custom Code for Updating Pay History for 210 record
	***********************************/
	
	if @Custom = 'UPDPAYHIST'

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '';  --replace with custom code
	END



	/**********************************
	Custom Code for Gens to be included in 220 Data
	***********************************/
	
	if @Custom = 'CURGEN'

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '' ; --replace with custom code
	END


	/**********************************
	Custom Code for Updating PayData for 220 record
	***********************************/
	
	if @Custom = 'UPDPAYDATA'

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '';  --replace with custom code
	END



	/**********************************
	Custom Code for 220
	***********************************/


	if @Custom = '220'

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '' ; --replace with custom code
	END

		
	/**********************************
	Custom Code for 290
	***********************************/
	
	if @Custom = '290'

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '' ; --replace with custom code
	END


	/**********************************
	Custom Code for 140
	***********************************/
	
	if @Custom = '140'

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '';  --replace with custom code
	END




	/**********************************
	Custom Code for BENEFITS - 230 and 240 record types
	***********************************/

	if @Custom = 'BENEFITS'

	BEGIN

		-- call BDM

		INSERT INTO dbo.U_dsi_bdm_Configuration VALUES (@FormatCode, 'DedTypes', 'MED,DEN,VIS');
		INSERT INTO dbo.U_dsi_bdm_Configuration VALUES (@FormatCode, 'StartDateTime',@startdate);
		INSERT INTO dbo.U_dsi_bdm_Configuration VALUES (@FormatCode, 'EndDateTime',@enddate);
		INSERT INTO dbo.U_dsi_bdm_Configuration VALUES (@FormatCode, 'TermSelectionOption', 'AuditDate');

		EXEC dbo.dsi_bdm_sp_PopulateDeductionsTable @FormatCode;


		/********************************************
		CREATE TABLES FOR USE FOR 230 RECORD
		All fields are defined, ad the joins are defined
		may have to modify based on client needs - just a sample
		*********************************************/


		SELECT DISTINCT
			drvsubsort = cast('' as varchar(32)),
			drveeid = eeceeid,
			drvcoid = eeccoid,
			drvCoCode = drvcocode,
			drvSSN = eepssn,
			drvEmplID = drvEmplID,
			drvDivision = drvDivision,
			drvMasterRecord = 'N',
			drvBenEffDate = getdate(),
			drvNextOEDate =  cast(cast(case when substring(convert(varchar(10),getdate(),112),5,4) < = '1115' then
							  left(convert(varchar(10),getdate(),112),4) else left(convert(varchar(10),getdate(),112),4) + 1 end as char(4))
								+ '1101' as datetime),  
			drvMedAvail = 'Y',
			drvMedElig = case when eecdedgroupcode in ('HRLY', 'SLRY', 'NONEX', 'MIT') then 'Y' else 'N' end,
			drvMedEnroll = coalesce(med.enroll,'N'),
			drvMedCarrier = med.dedbenplanprovider,
			drvMedPolicy = med.ProCompanyID, 
			drvMedPhone = med.ProPhoneBusinessNumber, 
			drvIneligReason = case when eecdedgroupcode in ('HRLY', 'SLRY', 'NONEX', 'MIT') then '' else '03' end, 
			drvEligDate = space(10),
			drvStartdate = med.benstartdate,
			drvTermDate = space(10),
			drvLevel = med.benoption,
			drvDepCov = 'Y',
			drvCostAddDep = space(8),
			drvDepCount = cast(0 as int),
			drvGroup = med.ProBillingInfo,
			drvMedAddress1 = med.ProAddressLine1,
			drvMedAddress2 = med.ProAddressLine2,
			drvMedCity = med.ProAddressCity,
			drvMedState = med.ProAddressState,
			drvMedZipCode = med.ProAddressZipCode,
			drvMedCountry = med.ProAddressCountryCode,
			drvCobra = space(1),
			drvAnnInsCost = space(8),
			drvDenAvail = 'Y',
			drvDenElig = case when eecdedgroupcode in ('HRLY', 'SLRY', 'NONEX', 'MIT') then 'Y' else 'N' end,
			drvDenEnroll = coalesce(den.enroll,'N'),
			drvDenCarrier = den.DedBenPlanProvider,
			drvDenPolicy = den.ProCompanyID,
			drvDenPhone = den.ProPhoneBusinessNumber,
			drvVisAvail = 'Y',
			drvVisElig = case when eecdedgroupcode in ('HRLY', 'SLRY', 'NONEX', 'MIT') then 'Y' else 'N' end,
			drvVisEnroll = coalesce(vis.enroll,'N'),
			drvVisCarrier = vis.DedBenPlanProvider,
			drvVisPolicy = vis.ProCompanyID,
			drvVisPhone = vis.ProPhoneBusinessNumber

		INTO dbo.U_EEQFX_230_drvtbl
		FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_202_drvtbl 
		JOIN EmpComp WITH (NOLOCK)ON drvcoid = eeccoid AND drveeid = eeceeid 
		JOIN Emppers WITH (NOLOCK)ON eepeeid = eeceeid
		left join (select eedeeid eeid, eedcoid coid, eeddedcode dedcode, 'Y' enroll,
			case when EedBenOption = 'EE' then '01'
				when EedBenOption = 'EECHLD' then '04'
				when EedBenOption = 'EESP' then '03'
				when EedBenOption = 'EEZDP' then '28'
				Else '05' end benoption, eedbenstartdate benstartdate,
			   probillinginfo, proaddressline1, proaddressline2, proaddresscity, proaddressstate, proaddresszipcode, proaddresscountrycode,
			   procompanyid, prophonebusinessnumber,dedbenplanprovider
			from dbo.U_dsi_bdm_EmpDeductions
			left join provider on proprovidercode = dedbenplanprovider
			where deddedtype = 'MED' and eedformatcode = @formatcode and eedvalidforexport = 'Y' and eedbenstopdate is null) med on med.eeid = drveeid and med.coid = drvcoid
		left join (select eedeeid eeid, eedcoid coid, eeddedcode dedcode, 'Y' enroll,
				procompanyid, prophonebusinessnumber, dedbenplanprovider
			from dbo.U_dsi_bdm_EmpDeductions
			left join provider on proprovidercode = dedbenplanprovider
			where deddedtype = 'DEN' and eedformatcode = @formatcode and eedvalidforexport = 'Y' and eedbenstopdate is null) den on den.eeid = drveeid and den.coid = drvcoid
		left join (select eedeeid eeid, eedcoid coid, eeddedcode dedcode, 'Y' enroll,
				procompanyid, prophonebusinessnumber, dedbenplanprovider
			from dbo.U_dsi_bdm_EmpDeductions
			left join provider on proprovidercode = dedbenplanprovider
			where deddedtype = 'VIS' and eedformatcode = @formatcode and eedvalidforexport = 'Y' and eedbenstopdate is null) vis on vis.eeid = drveeid and vis.coid = drvcoid
		where coalesce(med.enroll,den.enroll,vis.enroll) is not null;




		/********************************************
		CREATE TABLES FOR USE FOR 240 RECORD

		All fields are defined, ad the joins are defined
		may have to add fields to joins

		*********************************************/

		SELECT DISTINCT
			drvsubsort = cast('' as varchar(32)),
			drveeid = drveeid,
			drvcoid = drvcoid,
			drvCoCode = drvcocode,
			drvSSN = drvssn,
			drvEmplID = drvEmplID,
			drvDivision = drvDivision,
			drvDepSSN = conssn,
			drvDepNameFirst = connamefirst,
			drvDepnameLast = connamelast,
			drvDepNameMiddle = substring(connamemiddle, 1, 1),
			drvDepDateofBirth = condateofbirth

		INTO dbo.U_EEQFX_240_drvtbl
		FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_230_drvtbl
		JOIN Emppers WITH (NOLOCK)ON eepeeid = drveeid
		join dbo.U_dsi_bdm_DepDeductions on drveeid = dbneeid and drvcoid = dbncoid and dbnbenstopdate is null
							and deddedtype = 'MED'
		JOIN contacts WITH (NOLOCK) ON coneeid = dbneeid and dbndeprecid = consystemid
		Where dbnformatcode = @formatcode and dbnvalidforexport = 'Y';


		-- count dependents with Medical Coverage
		select
			depeeid = drveeid,
			depcoid = drvcoid,
			depcount = count(*)

		INTO dbo.U__EEQFX_240cnt_drvtbl
		FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_240_drvtbl
		group by drveeid,drvcoid;

		-- udpate count into 230 records

		Update dbo.U_EEQFX_230_drvtbl
		set  drvdepcount = depcount
		from dbo.U_EEQFX_230_drvtbl
		join dbo.U_EEQFX_240cnt_drvtbl on drveeid  = depeeid and drvcoid = depcoid;

	END



	/**********************************
	Custom Code for I-9 - 350, 160, 162, 372 record types
	***********************************/

	if @Custom = 'I-9'

	BEGIN


		/**********************************
		Create 350 Records
		***********************************/
		--  Code  below , fields are defined but values may need updated
		
		SELECT DISTINCT
			drvsubsort = cast('' as varchar(32)),
			drveeid = eeceeid,
			drvCoCode = drvcocode,   -- must match 200/202 record
			drvssn = eepssn,
			drvemplid = drvEmplID,	-- must match 200/202 record
			drvlocation = eecorglvl1 + '-' + rtrim(cmpcompanycode) + eeclocation,   -- must be unique by location code by FEIN
			drvaction = 'A',
			drvlocationsource = Space(32),	-- not use
			drvfein = replace(cmpFedTaxID,'-',''),
			drvlocationnumber = loccode,
			drvorglvl1 = eecorglvl1,
			drvTCIID = dbo.dsi_fnVariable('EEQFX', 'vTCIID')

		INTO dbo.U_EEQFX_350_drvtbl
		FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_202_drvtbl 
		JOIN empcomp ON eeceeid = drveeid AND eeccoid = drvcoid
		JOIN location WITH (NOLOCK) ON Eeclocation = LocCode
		JOIN emppers ON eepeeid = eeceeid
		JOIN company ON cmpcoid = drvcoid
		where Locaddresscountry = 'USA';


			-- Code commented out, if client is removing old locations this is used to send the deletes
			--	will need to update logic for which locations to remove based on fields being used for location

			/*****
			SELECT DISTINCT
				drvsubsort = cast('' as varchar(32)),
				drveeid = eeceeid,
				drvCoCode = drvcocode,   -- must match 200/202 record
				drvssn = eepssn,
				drvemplid = drvEmplID	-- must match 200/202 record
				drvlocation = eecorglvl1 + '-' + rtrim(cmpcompanycode) + eeclocation,   -- must be unique by location code by FEIN
				drvaction = 'D',
				drvlocationsource = Space(32),	-- not used
				drvfein = replace(cmpFedTaxID,'-',''),
				drvlocationnumber = loccode,
				drvorglvl1 = eecorglvl1,
				drvTCIID = dbo.dsi_fnVariable('EEQFX', 'vTCIID')

			INTO dbo.U_EEQFX_350_drvtbl
			FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_202_drvtbl 
			join empcomp on eeceeid = drveeid and eeccoid = drvcoid
			JOIN location WITH (NOLOCK) ON eeclocation = LocCode
			JOIN emppers ON eepeeid = eeceeid
			JOIN company ON cmpcoid = eeccoid
			where not exists(select 1 from dbo.U_EEQFX_350_drvtbl
						where drveeid = eeceeid and drvlocation = eecorglvl1 + '-' + rtrim(cmpcompanycode) + eeclocation)
				and Locaddresscountry = 'USA'

			*******/

	/**********************************
	Create I-9 Location Records
		These are in a separate file
		They will include a header (recordset 97), 160 record (recordset 16), trailer (recordset 98)
		And may include 162 recordset(90), 372 record types (recordset(91)
	***********************************/

	--   fields are defined but values may need updating
	

	/**********************************
	Create Header for I-9 Location File
	***********************************/
	if (select 1 from u_dsi_sqlclauses where rtrim(formatcode) = 'EEQFX' 
			and rtrim(isnull(left(whereclause,6),'')) <> 'IGNORE'
			and rtrim(recordset) = 'D16') = 1

	BEGIN

		Select
			 drvVersion = dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@FormatCode,'vVersiON')
			,drvSourceID = dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@FormatCode,'vSourceID')
			,drvSourceType = dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@FormatCode,'vSourceType')
			,drvSubmissionType = space(1)
			,drvSourceService = space(5)
			,drvEmplidOnly = space(1)

		INTO dbo.U_EEQFX_I9LocHeader_drvtbl;



		/**********************************
		Create 160 Record
		***********************************/

		Select distinct
			drvsubsort = cast('' as varchar(32)),
			drveeid = space(15),
			drvCoCode = drvCoCode,
			drvlocation = drvLocation,
			drvlocationname = rtrim(drvorglvl1)+ '-' + rtrim(drvlocation) + ' - ' + locdesc,
			drvlocaddressline1 = locaddressline1,
			drvlocaddressline2 = locaddressline2,
			drvlocaddresscity = locaddresscity,
			drvlocaddressstate = locaddressstate,
			drvlocaddresszipcode = CASE WHEN LEN(locaddresszipcode) = 5 THEN locaddresszipcode
									WHEN LEN(locaddresszipcode) = 9 THEN SUBSTRING(locaddresszipcode, 1, 5) + '-' + SUBSTRING(locaddresszipcode, 6, 4) END,

			drvlocphone1 = locphonemainnumber,
			drvlocphone2 = space(10),
			drvlocfax = locphonefaxnumber,
			drvlocemailaddress = space(64),
			drvlocgroup = space(1),
			drvrever1email = space(64),
			drvrever2email = space(64),
			drvbp1email = space(64),
			drvbp2email = space(64),
			drvbasicpilotind = 'Y',
			drvhirecodeind = space(1),
			drvivrind = space(1),
			drvlocactive = CASE WHEN LocISInactive = 'Y' THEN 'N' else 'Y' end,			
			drvfein = drvfein,
			drvlocativedate = locimportcode,
			drvlocinactivedate = locinactivedate,
			drvTCIID = drvTCIID

		INTO dbo.U_EEQFX_160_drvtbl
		FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_350_drvtbl
		JOIN location WITH (NOLOCK) ON drvlocationnumber = LocCode;

	END



	/**********************************
	Create 162 Record (Recordset 90) - Used for Location Hierarchy
		logic will need modified in the parent_loc_code and the from clause
		to select the correct group for each location
	***********************************/

	if (select 1 from u_dsi_sqlclauses where rtrim(formatcode) = 'EEQFX' 
			and rtrim(isnull(left(whereclause,6),'')) <> 'IGNORE'
			and rtrim(recordset) = 'D90') = 1

	BEGIN

		select distinct
			drvsubsort = cast('' as varchar(32)),
			drveeid = space(15),
			cocode = drvcocode,
			location_code = drvlocation,
			parent_loc_code = '?'			-- need to know how to group locations

		into dbo.U_EEQFX_162_drvtbl
		from dbo.U_EEQFX_160_drvtbl;


		/**********************************
		Also will need to create a 160 Record for each parent_loc_code
			Need to modify logic to figure out how to populate the fields
		***********************************/

		insert INTO dbo.U_EEQFX_160_drvtbl
		Select distinct
			drvsubsort = cast('' as varchar(32)),
			drveeid = space(15),
			drvCoCode = drvCoCode,
			drvlocation = parent_loc_code,
			drvlocationname = '??',
			drvlocaddressline1 = '',
			drvlocaddressline2 = '',
			drvlocaddresscity = '',
			drvlocaddressstate = '',
			drvlocaddresszipcode = '', 
			drvlocphone1 = '',
			drvlocphone2 = space(10),
			drvlocfax = '',
			drvlocemailaddress = space(64),
			drvlocgroup = 'G',
			drvrever1email = space(64),
			drvrever2email = space(64),
			drvbp1email = space(64),
			drvbp2email = space(64),
			drvbasicpilotind = space(1),
			drvhirecodeind = space(1),
			drvivrind = space(1),
			drvlocactive = '',			
			drvfein = '',		--replace(cmpFedTaxID,'-',''),
			drvlocativedate = null,
			drvlocinactivedate = null,
			drvTCIID = drvtciid		--drvTCIID

		FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_162_drvtbl;

	END

	/**********************************
	Create 372 Record (Recordset 91) - Used for Multi-User Auth
		We will not use the 370, but will always send the 'NONE' first so it removes all locations
			and adds current ones
		Code needs updated for logic on values to populate and joins

	If using this record the initialsort must be set to drvssn and the subsort to drvsort
	***********************************/

	if (select 1 from u_dsi_sqlclauses where rtrim(formatcode) = 'EEQFX' 
			and rtrim(isnull(left(whereclause,6),'')) <> 'IGNORE'
			and rtrim(recordset) = 'D91') = 1

	BEGIN

		-- send NONE record first to remove user security from all locations

		select distinct
			drvsubsort = cast(1 as varchar(32)),  -- used so nones sort first
			drveeid = drveeid,
			drvCoCode = drvcocode,	-- must match 202 record
			drvssn = drvssn,		-- must match 202 record
			drvuserid = drvuserid,	--must match 202 record
			drvuserrole = cast('None' as varchar(24)),
			drvI9location = space(32),  -- location code from 160 (may be a group location)
			drvhrxrole = cast('None' as varchar(50))  -- valid values on Statement of Work, 

		Into dbo.U_EEQFX_372_drvtbl
		FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_372prior_drvtbl;



		-- now send correct records
		select distinct
			drvsubsort = cast(2 as varchar(32)),
			drveeid = emp.drveeid,
			drvCoCode = emp.drvcocode,	-- must match 202 record
			drvssn = emp.drvssn,		-- must match 202 record
			drvuserid = emp.drvuserid,	--must match 202 record
			drvuserrole = 'LOCATIONMANAGER',
			drvI9location = drvlocation, -- location code from 350 or 160 (may be a group location)
			drvhrxrole = 'NONE'  -- valid values on Statement of Work, must be the same for an employee for all their locations, 

		Into dbo.U_EEQFX_372_drvtbl
		FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_202_drvtbl emp
		join rbsquallist ql on drveeid = myeeid
		join rbsroles rl on rl.rolid =  ql.roleid and rolname in ('MGRSTORE','MGRGM')
		join rbsqualifiers on qalroleid = ql.roleid and qalfield = 'eecorglvl1' and qaluserid = userid
		join dbo.U_EEQFX_350_drvtbl I9 on qalvalue = drvorglvl1;


		-- may need more inserts based on client

		--save 372 records 
		IF OBJECT_ID ('U_EEQFX_372prior_drvtbl') IS NOT NULL
			DROP TABLE dbo.U_EEQFX_372prior_drvtbl;

		select * into dbo.U_EEQFX_372prior_drvtbl from dbo.U_EEQFX_372_drvtbl;

	END


END  -- I9 Processing


	/**********************************
	Custom Code for FINAL Updates
	***********************************/


	if @Custom = 'FINAL'

	BEGIN
	set @dummy = '';  --replace with custom code
	END


/*******
Add any testing statements here


********/

GO


/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[dsi_sp_AfterCollect_EEQFX]    Script Date: 03/28/2016 13:11:18 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [dbo].[dsi_sp_AfterCollect_EEQFX]
as

/*** Please note some clients have different Equifax company codes (drvcocode). 
 In such case data needs to be summed within the Equifax company. Also, client
may have different files created based on Equifax company. 
 There may also be override parameters or translations in u_dsi_translation_v2 to use.
If recordsets are in the translations, they are to not be processed, so query should not create 
records in the table.

A separate file(s) must be created if a client uses the I9 Location reporting

There is a variable in the configuration to indicate if separate files are need by equifax company

Revision History
-----------------
Updated By		Date		Desc   
Lynn Manning	10/06/2015	Update file grouping
Lynn Manning	03/17/2016	Remove function dsi_fnGetExportPath as not all new databases have that installed
								and use dsi_fnVariable to get file path instead


*************/
BEGIN

    DECLARE @FormatCode char(10);
    SELECT  @FormatCode = 'EEQFX';

    DECLARE  @ExportCode char(10)
			,@exportpath  varchar(100)
			,@filename  varchar(200)
			,@scmd varchar(4000)
			,@testing char(1)
			,@vUseSpecChars char(1)
			,@vsplitFiles char(1)
			,@vMainCoCode varchar(10) ;

	SET @vUseSpecChars = dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@formatcode,'vUseSpecChars');
	SET @vSplitFiles = dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@formatcode,'vSplitFiles');
	SET @vMainCoCode = dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@formatcode,'vCoCode')  ;

    DECLARE
		@v_Servername varchar (32),
		@dbname  varchar (30),
		@query  varchar (4000),
		@Result  int,
		@eqfxco  varchar(20),
		@filetype  varchar(5);


	-- THESE VARIABLES ADDED TO ALLOW MORE AUTOMATION TO PROCESS
	SELECT	@v_ServerName = '"' + rtrim(@@SERVERNAME) + '"',
			@dbname = rtrim(db_name()),
			@exportcode = exportcode
	from dbo.U_dsi_Parameters with (nolock)
	where FormatCode = @FormatCode;

	-- split files if needed  also send with special characters if required


	-- File Path
	IF @ExportCode LIKE 'TEST%'
	BEGIN
		SELECT @ExportPath = ltrim(rtrim(IsNull(dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@FormatCode, 'TestPath'),'')));
	END;
	
	IF @ExportCode IN ('ONDEMAND','SCHEDULED')
	BEGIN
		SELECT @ExportPath = CASE WHEN dbo.dsi_fnVariable('EEQFX','vFileType') = 'T' THEN ltrim(rtrim(IsNull(dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@FormatCode, 'TestPath'),'')))
				  	WHEN dbo.dsi_fnVariable('EEQFX','vFileType') = 'P' THEN ltrim(rtrim(IsNull(dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@FormatCode, 'ExportPath'),'')))
					END;
	END;

	IF ISNULL(@ExportPath,'') = '' 
	BEGIN
		SELECT @ExportPath = ltrim(rtrim(IsNull(dbo.dsi_fnVariable(@FormatCode, 'ExportPath'),'')));
	END;
	
	
	IF RIGHT(@ExportPath,1) <> '\'
	BEGIN
		SELECT @ExportPath = RTRIM(@ExportPath) + '\' ;
	END;
    		
	-- select @ExportPath = ltrim(rtrim(IsNull(dbo.dsi_fnGetExportPath(@FormatCode, @exportcode),'')))  -- commented out 3/28/16 


	BEGIN

		DECLARE EQFXfile CURSOR FAST_FORWARD FOR

		SELECT distinct 
			case when isnull(@vSplitFiles,'N') = 'N' then rtrim(@vMainCoCode) else rtrim(subsort2) end, -- @eqfxco
			case when coalesce(transvalue,dbo.dsi_fnVariable('EEQFX','vFileType')) = 'T' or @exportcode like 'TEST%' then 'TST' else 'PROD' end 
		FROM dbo.U_EEQFX_File
		LEFT JOIN dbo.u_dsi_translations_v2 ftype with (nolock) 
				on ftype.formatcode = @formatcode and ftype.Transcode = 'vFileType' and ftype.srcvalue = rtrim(subsort2) and isnull(@vSplitFiles,'N') = 'Y'
		WHERE LEFT(RecordSet ,1) = 'D'

		OPEN EQFXfile

		FETCH NEXT FROM EQFXFile INTO @eqfxco, @filetype

		WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
		BEGIN

		SELECT @Query = 'select top 200000000  Data  from ' + @dbname + '.dbo.U_EEQFX_File with (nolock) ' +
				'where recordset not in (''H97'',''D16'',''D90'',''D91'',''T98'') and (left(recordset,1) in(''H'',''T'') or rtrim(Subsort2) = ''' 
				+  @eqfxco +  ''' or isnull(''' + @vSplitFiles +  ''',''N'') = ''N'' )' + 
          ' order by case substring(RecordSet,1,1) when ''H'' then 1 when ''D'' then 2 else 3 end, Subsort2, InitialSort, cast(substring(RecordSet,2,2) as int),subsort'

		select @filename = @eqfxco + @filetype + 'in.msf'

		select @sCmd = 'BCP "'  +  @query + '" QueryOut "' + @ExportPath + @FileName + '" -o "' + @ExportPath + 'ExportLog.txt"' + 
						' -S ' + @v_ServerName + ' -T -c -t' + case when isnull(@vUseSpecChars,'N') = 'Y' then ' -C RAW' 
						else '' end

		print @scmd

		EXEC @Result = master.dbo.xp_cmdshell @sCmd , NO_OUTPUT


		----------
		-- Build I9 Location File if 160 record being used
		----------
		
		IF (	select 1 from u_dsi_sqlclauses where rtrim(formatcode) = 'EEQFX' 
				and rtrim(isnull(left(whereclause,6),'')) <> 'IGNORE'
				and rtrim(recordset) = 'D16') = 1
		BEGIN

			select @Query = 'select top 200000000  Data  from ' + @dbname + '.dbo.U_EEQFX_File with (nolock) ' +
				'where recordset in (''H97'',''D16'',''D90'',''D91'',''T98'') and (left(recordset,1) in(''H'',''T'') or rtrim(Subsort2) = ''' 
				+  @eqfxco +  ''' or isnull(''' + @vSplitFiles +  ''',''N'') = ''N'' )' + 
				' order by case substring(RecordSet,1,1) when ''H'' then 1 when ''D'' then 2 else 3 end, Subsort2, InitialSort, cast(substring(RecordSet,2,2) as int),subsort'

			print @query

			select @filename =   @eqfxco + case when @filetype = 'TST' then '_i9test_' else '_i9prod_' end 
									+ replace(convert(varchar(10),getdate(),101),'/','')
									+ '_userloc.i9'

			select @sCmd = 'bcp "' + @query + '" queryout "' + @ExportPath + @FileName 
							+ '" -o "' + @ExportPath + 'ExportLog.txt"' + ' -T -S' + @v_ServerName + ' -c -t '


			EXEC @Result = master.dbo.xp_cmdshell @sCmd  --, NO_OUTPUT
			
		END

		FETCH NEXT FROM EQFXfile INTO @eqfxco , @filetype
	
	END 

	CLOSE EQFXfile
	DEALLOCATE EQFXfile
	END

END




GO
